2026-04-24 / CCL→ND: solicitor approval required (no silent uploads) / Nothing goes to NetDocuments without an explicit solicitor click. Removed two silent paths: (1) the `CCL_AUTO_UPLOAD_ND=1` autopilot branch in `/api/ccl/service/run` is now a no-op that logs `CCL.NdUpload.Skipped.AwaitingApproval` — env flag preserved as a deprecation shim so staging can't silently re-enable it; (2) the "CCL Uploaded to NetDocuments" step in the matter-opening pipeline is removed. Matter opening now ends at CCL generation. Solicitors approve from one of two entry points, both converging on the same review rail (`openHomeCclReview` CustomEvent → PreviewStep → `handleUploadNd`): (a) "Review & send CCL" on the matter-opening completion screen (MatterOpenedHandoff), or (b) a `review-ccl` hub_todo on Home. The todo is now always emitted after generation — flagged drafts get "Review CCL · N flagged", clean drafts get "Approve CCL upload". On successful ND upload, `/api/ccl-ops/upload-nd` auto-closes the matching todo via `reconcileAllByRef`. Tightened the MatterOpenedHandoff subline to make the contract explicit and added the same note to the demo-mode strip.  In Everyone mode multiple firm-wide to-do cards rendered in the bar and each `PanelActionRow` held its own `expanded` boolean, so users could open every tray simultaneously and the expansion panes stacked into an overflow mess. 2026-04-24 / Dev boot wave 2: frontend compile cuts + boot timing / Layered on top of today's Key Vault cache work. Frontend now defaults to `GENERATE_SOURCEMAP=false` and `DISABLE_ESLINT_PLUGIN=true` inside `dev-all-with-logs.mjs` — webpack cold compile drops ~30–60s (source map generation + ESLint pass removed; VS Code's ESLint extension still lints in-editor, TS errors still surface via `TSC_COMPILE_ON_ERROR=true`, and browser devtools still get cheap eval source maps). Can be overridden by exporting the env var. Backend now emits `[boot-timing] +NNNNms <label>` landmarks at appinsights/env/core-utils/hydration/routes/listen milestones when `HELIX_BOOT_TIMING` is set (default on for `dev:all`, silence with `HELIX_BOOT_TIMING=0`) — this lets us see which phase is eating budget across restarts without guessing. No behaviour change in production (`NODE_ENV=production` always skips both). (~ server/index.js, ~ tools/dev-all-with-logs.mjs)

2026-04-24 / Faster dev boot: local Key Vault cache + az token pre-warm / Two changes together cut `npm run dev:all` cold-boot from ~260s to ~100s on repeat boots (and ~130s on first-of-day). 1) `server/utils/getSecret.js` now persists successfully-resolved secrets to `.secrets-cache.json` (gitignored, 7-day TTL, 0600 perms, dev-only — disabled in production and when `HELIX_NO_SECRET_CACHE=1`). Subsequent boots skip the Key Vault round-trip entirely, saving ~5–200s depending on az token freshness. 2) `tools/dev-all-with-logs.mjs` pre-warms the az CLI token for `https://vault.azure.net` in the background before spawning the backend, so `@azure/identity` never stalls on a stale token. Also bumped the backend port-wait from 120s → 240s so the orchestrator doesn't give up early on genuinely slow first-run boots. Added `.secrets-cache.json` to `.gitignore`. (~ server/utils/getSecret.js, ~ tools/dev-all-with-logs.mjs, ~ .gitignore)

2026-04-24 / Single loading cue / The `!dataReady` global shimmer strip (above the scroll region) and the per-Suspense `ThemedSuspenseFallback` strip both rendered at 2px during boot and stacked into a visible 4px underline on the filter bar. Gated the per-Suspense strip behind `dataReady` — during boot, the global bar is the single cue (no stacking); post-boot, the Suspense fallback is the single cue when a not-yet-prefetched chunk is arriving. Either way, exactly one 2px strip is visible at any moment. (~ src/app/App.tsx)

2026-04-24 / Snappier tab switching (chunk prefetch) / Two low-cost changes to remove the network leg from the tab-switch critical path without adding mount/render work: (1) `CustomTabs` now fires `onTabWarm` on `onPointerDown` + `onTouchStart` in addition to hover/focus — on desktop the chunk starts downloading ~50–100ms before `click` fires (the gap between pointerdown and pointerup-then-click), and on touch devices hover never fires at all so this is the first signal we get. (2) The idle `warmNavigationChunks` effect on Home (runs 4s after Home mount via `requestIdleCallback`) now prefetches `Instructions`, `Reporting`, and `Roadmap` chunks in addition to `Enquiries`/`Matters`. Chunks only — no component mount, no subscriptions opened. `warmTabByKey` also now handles `roadmap`. Net: first visit to any tab should land on a cached chunk, making the Suspense shimmer invisible in the common case. (~ src/app/App.tsx, ~ src/app/styles/CustomTabs.tsx)

2026-04-24 / Stop voiding content behind loading bars / Two fixes so partial data is visible while the rest loads, instead of the whole viewport being replaced by a tiny shimmer bar: (1) Removed the `!dataReady` wipe in `App.tsx` that replaced the entire tab content area with a centred 120×2 shimmer block until both `teamsContext` and `userData` resolved — tabs now render immediately and each handles its own empty/loading state internally (matters already guards on `isLoading && length === 0`, home/enquiries already render skeletons). The thin top loading bar (`!dataReady` strip above the scroll region) remains as the single global "still working" cue. (2) Slimmed `ThemedSuspenseFallback` from a 200-px-minHeight centred block to a 2px top shimmer strip so first-time lazy tab chunk loads no longer produce a floor-to-ceiling void — surrounding chrome (navigator, header, keep-alive siblings) stays visible. Added `role="status"` + `aria-label` for screen readers. (~ src/app/App.tsx)

2026-04-24 / CCL — Review CCL pickup skips intro/generation screens / Clicking the `Review CCL` immediate-action chip on Home (or the CCL status pill in the Matters table) was re-showing the compile → draft → pressure-test intro before landing on the review rail, even when the CCL was already drafted and pressure-tested. 2026-04-23 / CCL pipeline telemetry — AutoFill + PressureTest lifecycle events / Phase C1 of CCL_REVIEW_LANDING_TERSER_INTRO_START_FROM_SCRATCH_AFFORDANCE_PIPELINE_TOASTING. Previously only `CCL.AutoFill.Started/Skipped` and `CCL.OverrideRerun.*` were instrumented — AutoFill completions/failures and the entire pressure-test lifecycle were invisible in App Insights, so we couldn't measure generation latency, confidence distribution, PT flag rate, or detect Safety-Net failures without inferring from the absence of data. Added `CCL.AutoFill.Completed` (fieldCount, confidence, durationMs, unresolvedCount, stage, override), `CCL.AutoFill.Failed` (error, phase, override), `CCL.PressureTest.Started` (fieldCount, silent), `CCL.PressureTest.Completed` (fieldCount, flaggedCount, durationMs, silent) and `CCL.PressureTest.Failed` (error, fieldCount, durationMs, silent). No UX changes, no behaviour change — foundation for Phase C2–C4 toast/rail work. (~ src/components/modern/OperationsDashboard.tsx)

2026-04-23 / Attendance save — fix "Saving..." hang when dev proxy is slow / "All WFH → Submit" appeared stuck: the server returned 200 in ~460ms via curl but the browser fetch through CRA's dev proxy took 6s+ (HTTP/1 connection pool starved by multiple long-lived SSE streams). `saveAttendance` had no timeout so a slow fetch could hang longer than the child modal's 15s safety timer, which reset the Submit label but never closed the modal — leaving the user looking at a dead-looking dialog. Fix: (1) wrap the `fetch` in `saveAttendance` with an `AbortController` + 20s timeout so the client gives up before the user does; (2) `PersonalAttendanceConfirm.handleSave` now also calls `onClose()` in the catch branch so an error always releases the modal; (3) extended the safety timer to 30s and made it fire a toast + close the modal if it ever triggers (was previously silent). Playwright-verified: modal closes at t=6s with success toast, two weeks saved (responses 200+200). (~ src/tabs/home/Home.tsx, ~ src/tabs/home/PersonalAttendanceConfirm.tsx)

2026-04-23 / Unblock more stuck lazy imports — AttendancePortal, TeamInsight, CallsAndNotes / Same hang as Request Leave and Personal Attendance: `React.lazy(() => import(...))` never resolved in this dev bundle (craco custom splitChunks/cache skip chunk emission in dev), so Home's Attendance today + Team Leave panels stayed on skeleton and OperationsDashboard was stuck on "Loading Call Centre…". Surrounding `<Suspense>` wrappers left in place (no-op when children don't throw — safer than deleting). Playwright-verified: Call Centre list, Attendance today, and Team Leave all render on load. (~ src/tabs/home/Home.tsx, ~ src/components/modern/OperationsDashboard.tsx)

2026-04-23 / Unify attendance self-click + unblock PersonalAttendanceConfirm modal / Two linked issues: (1) the "Attendance" quick action on Home appeared broken — the BespokePanel shell opened but the body was perma-stuck on "Loading attendance data..." (the ModalSkeleton Suspense fallback). 2026-04-23 / Approve Leave modal — open even when empty; Book Leave radius cleanup / "Approve Annual Leave" quick action felt broken — clicking it did nothing when the queue was empty because `handleApproveLeaveClick` in Home.tsx had an early-return guard `if (approvalsNeeded.length > 0)` that silently no-op'd. `AnnualLeaveApprovals` already renders a tidy "All clear — No pending leave requests to review" empty state, so the guard was gratuitous. 2026-04-23 / Personal attendance modal — brand polish + save-hang fix / Attendance confirmation modal was (a) off-brand (stray `borderRadius: 3/4`, `borderRadius: '2px'/'3px'/'4px'`, non-canonical warm-orange RGB `255,183,77` / `255,152,0`, body text hardcoded `#374151`/`#F3F4F6`/`#E5E7EB`/`#9CA3AF`) and (b) perceived as "stuck on saving" — the API returns in ~460ms but if `onClose()` or the parent's optimistic update threw mid-flight the `saving` flag could linger. Changes: all stray radii collapsed to `0`; warm-orange rgba pinned to the canonical helper `rgba(255,140,0,…)` matching `colours.orange` (`#FF8C00`); body text swapped to `colours.dark.text` / `colours.light.text` / `colours.greyText` / `colours.subtleGrey`; `STATUS_CONFIG.away` + `STATUS_CONFIG.unset` colours moved off raw greys onto tokens. Save flow hardened: re-entry guard (`if (saving) return`), skip weeks with no day statuses (prevents 400 on empty), reset `saving` BEFORE `onClose()` so the button always visibly resets, `try/catch` around `onClose()` + toast, and a 15s safety timer that force-resets `saving` if a promise never resolves. Also removed 6 verbose `console.log` breadcrumbs from the save path. (~ src/tabs/home/PersonalAttendanceConfirm.tsx)

2026-04-23 / Fix refresh-hang on skeletons — shared SSE registry / Root cause of "first boot fine, refresh hangs on skeletons for 2–3s": Chrome caps HTTP/1.1 EventSource at **6 connections per origin**, but Home opens 10+ distinct stream URLs on mount (`/api/enquiries-unified/stream`, `/api/data-operations/stream`, `/api/attendance/attendance/stream`, `/api/attendance/annual-leave/stream`, `/api/future-bookings/stream`, `/api/outstanding-balances/stream`, `/api/ops-queue/stream`, `/api/doc-workspace/stream`, `/api/matters/stream`, `/api/home-metrics/stream`) plus **CallsAndNotes was opening a second connection to `/api/data-operations/stream`** via a raw `new EventSource`. On first boot no sockets exist; on refresh, surplus streams stalled until the prior TCP sockets released (~2-3s), which is exactly the hydration lag the telemetry strip was showing. **Fix**: `useRealtimeChannel` now uses a module-level per-URL connection registry (`Map<url, SharedConnection>`) — when multiple hook instances (or multiple components) subscribe to the same URL, they share one underlying `EventSource` via refcount. Each subscriber registers its own event listener + status listener; closing the last subscriber closes the shared connection. Public API unchanged. Also migrated CallsAndNotes' `data-ops.synced` subscription from raw `new EventSource` to `useRealtimeChannel`, so it deduplicates with Home's existing subscription and frees one of the 6 SSE slots. Net: Home should now open ~6-7 unique EventSources instead of 10-11, keeping the browser under the per-origin cap even during a reload overlap window. (~ src/hooks/useRealtimeChannel.ts, ~ src/components/modern/CallsAndNotes.tsx)

(~ src/tabs/home/AttendancePortal.css, ~ src/tabs/home/HomeSkeletons.tsx, - src/tabs/home/AwayInsight.tsx, - src/tabs/home/AttendanceInsight.tsx, - src/tabs/home/Attendance.tsx, - src/tabs/home/EnhancedAttendanceNew.tsx, - src/tabs/home/WeeklyAttendanceView.tsx)

2026-04-15 / Fix outstanding balances status query aliases / Outstanding balances status now uses SQL-safe snake_case summary aliases so the Finance Data Centre status card no longer 500s on SQL Server with "Incorrect syntax near the keyword 'rowCount'". (~ server/routes/outstandingBalances.js)

2026-04-15 / Materialise outstanding balances in Data Hub / Outstanding balances now sync into a Core Data table with status and reconcile endpoints, runtime reads go table-first with live fallback, and Data Centre Finance exposes freshness, sync, reconcile, and preview controls for the dataset. (~ server/routes/outstandingBalances.js, ~ server/routes/dataOperations.js, ~ src/tabs/Reporting/DataCentre.tsx)

2026-04-15 / Render-level compile-stage safety net / Compile-stage CCL matters now have a render-time safety net: if the modal opens and the callback-time seed didn't take (stale closure, race condition, or the draft fetch fired and failed), the render itself detects compile-stage + missing/errored draft, overrides `cached` in-place, and schedules a clean state update. This eliminates "Draft fetch failed — signal is aborted" permanently for compile-stage matters regardless of which code path opened the modal. Removed `cclMap` from `openCclLetterModal` deps to prevent stale-closure cascading. (~ src/components/modern/OperationsDashboard.tsx)

2026-04-15 / Fix compile-stage CCL draft fetch bypass / Compile-stage matters no longer attempt to fetch a saved draft that doesn't exist. The empty-draft seed and trace-resolved marker are now applied inside `openCclLetterModal` itself (using `getCanonicalCclStage`), so ALL entry points — pipeline steps, collapsed CTA, review request, flagged-field jumps — are covered. Previously the bypass only lived in `openCclWorkflowModal`, so direct `openCclLetterModal` callers would fire a 12s draft fetch that timed out with "signal is aborted", then crash the app when the render tried to use null fields. (~ src/components/modern/OperationsDashboard.tsx)

2026-04-15 / Resilient journey feed + specific note errors / Journey `buildSnapshot` now wraps all 5 data sources in individual `.catch()` handlers so a single SQL failure returns partial data with warnings instead of 500-ing the whole feed. Phone resolution capped at 30 per snapshot. Client shows error banner with retry button on journey fetch failure, and a warnings strip when sources are degraded. Attendance note generation returns distinct error codes (`NO_TRANSCRIPT`, `AI_UNAVAILABLE`, `AI_PARSE_ERROR`, `DB_ERROR`) instead of generic 500. Client parses codes and shows specific actionable messages. Save and ND upload failures now surface inline error text instead of being silent. (~ server/routes/home-journey.js, ~ server/routes/dubberCalls.js, ~ src/components/modern/CallsAndNotes.tsx)

2026-04-15 / Home fetches matters directly / Home now fetches the 50 most recent new-space matters directly via parallel fetch instead of waiting for the full app-level dataset. Server route supports `limit` param with `ORDER BY OpenDate DESC` and separate Redis cache key. Memory cache skipped for limited requests to avoid poisoning the full-dataset cache. (~ server/routes/mattersNewSpace.js, ~ src/tabs/home/Home.tsx)

2026-04-15 / Split Home and Matters onto new-space matters / Added a dedicated `/api/matters-new-space` route so Home and the default Matters tab now load from new-space matters only, while the mixed legacy route stays behind an admin-only fallback in Matters and Reporting remains untouched. (~ server/routes/mattersNewSpace.js, ~ server/index.js, ~ server/server.js, ~ src/index.tsx, ~ src/tabs/matters/Matters.tsx)

2026-04-15 / Fix silent failures in calls and notes / Attendance note generation and transcript fetching now surface errors instead of silently swallowing them. Note generation shows inline error message on failure (network, OpenAI timeout, missing transcript). Transcript fetch shows error with retry link. AI summaries now display even when sentence count is zero. (~ src/components/modern/CallsAndNotes.tsx)

2026-04-15 / Progressive ops queue rendering / Asana (external API) is now fetched independently from core ops queue data. Bank transfers, transactions, CCL dates, Stripe, and recent approvals render instantly while the Asana pipeline loads in the background. Asana server cache TTL bumped from 30s to 120s to reduce redundant external API calls. (~ src/components/modern/OperationsQueue.tsx, ~ server/routes/opsQueue.js)

2026-04-15 / Skip saved-review fetch for compile-stage matters / Compile-stage matters now bypass the draft and trace fetch entirely — the draft cache is seeded empty, the trace is marked resolved, and AI generation auto-triggers on open. Eliminates the 12-second timeout dance and "Loading saved review" copy for items that have no review yet. Launch overlay copy updated to show "Starting review generation" for the brief pre-generation window. (~ src/components/modern/OperationsDashboard.tsx)

2026-04-15 / Fix CCL review readiness mismatch / Fixed two bugs: (1) draft fetch failure wrote a truthy empty object into cache, poisoning subsequent opens and preventing retry — now writes null with a fetchError flag so the UI distinguishes fetch-failed from no-draft-exists and shows a retry button; (2) trace fetch failure did not mark as resolved, creating an infinite re-fetch loop that cycled "Checking for saved review data" indefinitely — now marks resolved on failure to break the loop. 2026-04-10 / Fix dev:all startup — webpack silent failure + Key Vault 75s delay / Root cause: webpack splitChunks config (vendor + fluentui) collided with CRA dev's single `bundle.js` filename — caused "Multiple chunks emit to same filename" error that silently killed compilation. Fix: only enable splitChunks in production. Also: switched Key Vault credential to AzureCliCredential in dev (was DefaultAzureCredential cycling 7 providers for 75s), saving 70s on every boot. Removed ForkTsCheckerWebpackPlugin in dev (IDE handles type checking). Fixed createLinePump to split on bare \r (react-scripts' terminal overwrite char). Added BROWSER=none and TSC_COMPILE_ON_ERROR=true to .env. Added frontend port-readiness announcement to dev-all-with-logs. Result: backend 5s (was 75s), frontend compiles and serves correctly. (~ craco.config.js, ~ server/utils/getSecret.js, ~ tools/dev-all-with-logs.mjs, ~ .env)

2026-04-09 / Performance: IIS caching + compression + vendor splitting + fetch dedup / CRITICAL FIX: IIS was serving static files directly, bypassing Express cache headers — all JS/CSS had no Cache-Control in production. Added IIS outbound rules: hashed assets in `/static/` get `immutable, max-age=1yr`, HTML gets `no-cache`. Enabled `urlCompression` for IIS-level gzip of static files. Removed `X-Powered-By` header. Fixed compression middleware creating new instance per-request (now singleton). Added webpack `splitChunks` for vendor + FluentUI — browsers cache vendor code independently across deploys. Removed ~170-line legacy duplicate attendance/annual-leave fetch that could race with the parallel fetch effect. (~ server/web.config, ~ server/index.js, ~ craco.config.js, ~ src/tabs/home/Home.tsx)

2026-03-25 / Fix Clio 401 thundering herd on startup / Team WIP warmup fired 64 parallel Clio API calls (32 members × 2 weeks), each independently retrying on 401 — flooding logs and hammering the OAuth endpoint. Root cause: getClioAccessToken() silently dropped the forceRefresh parameter. Fix: (1) pass forceRefresh through, (2) de-dup forced token refreshes via inflight promise so only one OAuth call happens, (3) remove per-request "Using Redis-cached credentials" log noise. Startup now produces 1 refresh log line instead of ~130. (~ server/routes/home-wip.js)

2026-03-25 / Fix concurrent cache-miss race condition / Added inflight request de-duplication to home-wip and home-enquiries routes. Barrel imports pull the entire ~1MB FluentUI v8 bundle; deep imports let webpack tree-shake unused modules. Type-only imports use `import type` for zero runtime cost. (~ 218 files across src/)

2026-03-10 / Fix pitched/instructed tabs with server-side stage derivation / Root cause: dbo.enquiries.stage is only ever 'new' or 'claimed' — never updated to 'pitched' or 'instructed'. The server query now LEFT JOINs Deals (for pitched status via PitchedDate) and Instructions (for instructed status via Stage/MatterId) to compute a derivedStage in SQL. Records with a Deal get stage='pitched'; records with an Instruction that has a MatterId or advanced stage get stage='instructed'. Increased client fetch limit from 12→80 so pitched/instructed records aren't cut off by the sort+slice. Pipeline dots now correctly reflect multi-dot progression for converted enquiries. (~ server/routes/home-enquiries.js, ~ src/components/modern/OperationsDashboard.tsx)

2026-03-02 / Fix pitched count to mean "of my enquiries, how many pitched" / Pitched count was independently counting deals by PitchedBy date, showing 6 when only 3 enquiries existed. 2026-03-02 / Fix pitched count inflated by duplicate deals per prospect / Homepage pitched count used `COUNT(CASE WHEN ... THEN 1 END)` which counted every deal row � multiple deals for the same InstructionRef inflated the number (e.g. BOD had 4 unique prospects but showed 6). Changed to `COUNT(DISTINCT CASE WHEN ... THEN InstructionRef END)` to count unique prospects pitched. (~ server/routes/home-enquiries.js)

2026-03-02 / Fix homepage enquiry count under-counting across dual databases / Homepage `/api/home-enquiries` used `Math.max(coreCount, instrCount)` to avoid double-counting migrated records, but this under-counts when unique enquiries exist in both DBs (e.g. Bianca had 2 in Core Data + 1 in Instructions = 3 total, homepage showed 2). Replaced with email-based deduplication: fetches email+date rows from both DBs, merges into a Set keyed by `email|date`, and counts the union. Also aligned Core Data date field from `Date_Created` to `Touchpoint_Date` to match the Management Dashboard (which uses the streaming endpoint's `Touchpoint_Date`). Removed dead `queryMainDbCounts`/`queryInstructionsDbCounts` functions. (~ server/routes/home-enquiries.js)

2026-03-02 / Fix Management Dashboard WIP missing for current week / Two bugs caused current-week WIP to disappear from the Management Dashboard: (1) **Cache coherence** � `cachedData.wip` stored raw SQL data (no current week) instead of the merged result; when ReportingHome remounted after tab switches, it initialised from the unmerged cache while `handleOpenDashboard` skipped refresh ("data <30min old"), so the Clio merge never re-ran. Fixed by persisting the merged result in `cachedData.wip`. (2) **Error swallowing** � `fetchWipClioCurrentWeek` in reporting.js caught all errors and returned an empty struct `{activities:[]}`, which the streaming route cached as 'ready' for 30 min. Changed to re-throw so the streaming handler sends `dataset-error` (not cached). Clio API confirmed working: 207 team-wide activities returned in 6.5s. (~ src/tabs/Reporting/ReportingHome.tsx, ~ server/routes/reporting.js, ~ server/routes/reporting-stream.js, ~ .github/instructions/ARCHITECTURE_DATA_FLOW.md)

2026-02-22 / Fix Outstanding Office Balances showing �0 / Two root causes: (1) Race condition � a useEffect fetching user-specific balances from /api/outstanding-balances/user/:entraId would overwrite richer firm-wide data delivered by the SSE stream, often replacing 127 records with 0. Removed the competing useEffect; the stream + client-side myOutstandingBalances filter is sufficient. (2) Premature zero � when normalizedMatters hadn't loaded yet, outstandingTotal returned 0 instead of null, so the card displayed �0 instead of the skeleton loading cue. Now returns null until matters are available, and isOutstandingLoading stays true until both data and matters are ready. Added ref guard (streamOutstandingReceivedRef) and diagnostic console logs. (~ src/tabs/home/Home.tsx)

2026-02-27 / Add commit sanity guard to data syncs / Both syncCollectedTime and syncWip now check insert-vs-delete ratio before committing. If Clio returned less than 30% of what was deleted (>50 rows), the transaction rolls back and preserves existing data instead of committing a net loss. Prevents data loss from partial Clio API responses, timeouts, or auth failures. (~ server/routes/dataOperations.js)
2026-02-27 / Wrap data sync DELETE+INSERT in SQL transactions / Both syncCollectedTime and syncWip now run DELETE + batch INSERT + dedup inside a single SQL transaction. If the process crashes mid-insertion (e.g. Azure App Service restart), the transaction rolls back and existing data is preserved instead of being permanently deleted. Previously DELETE committed immediately and partial INSERT left the table with missing rows. (~ server/routes/dataOperations.js)

LZ/Luke/localhost users had no Clio ID ? home-wip returned zeros ? triggered slow reporting fallback. Solution: removed email/initials from effect deps (derived from userData anyway), added Alex fallback logic to parallel fetch (matches handleRefreshTimeMetrics pattern), only trigger reporting fallback when truly needed (data exists but all zeros).
